   Jñānāmṛtasāra-Saṃhitā (also called "Nārada-Pañcarātra")	JQAna-amRta-sAra--SaMhitAH (alsaH callet "NArada--PaQcarAtra")
   śrī-nārada-pañca-rātram	SrI-nArada--paQca-rAtram
   prathamaika-rātre prathamo 'dhyāyaḥ	praTama-eka--rAtre praTamaH aDyAyaH
   oṃ namo bhagavate vāsudevāya	om namaH Bagavate vAsudevAya
   atha maṅgalācaraṇam	aTa maFgala-AcaraNam
   nārāyaṇaṃ namas kṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam /	nArAyaNam namaH kRtya naram ca-eva narottamam /
   devīṃ sarasvatīṃ caiva tato jayam udīrayet //	devIm sarasvatIm ca-eva tatas jayam udIrayet //
   gaṇeśa-śeṣa-brahmeśa-dineśa-pramukhāḥ surāḥ /	gaNeSa--Seza--brahma-ISa--dineSa--pramuKAH surAH /
   kumārādyāś ca munayaḥ siddhāś ca kapilādayaḥ // Jss_1,1.1 //	kumAra-AdyAH ca munayaH sidDAH ca kapila-AdayaH // JsH-_1,1.1 //
   lakṣmī sarasvatī durgā sāvitrī rādhikā parā /	lakzmI sarasvatI durgA sAvitrI rADikA parA /
   bhaktyā namanti yaṃ śaśvat taṃ namāmi parāt paraṃ // Jss_1,1.2 //	BaktyA namanti yam SaSvat tam namAmi parAt param // JsH-_1,1.2 //
   dhyāyante satataṃ santo yogino vaiṣṇavās tathā /	DyAyante satatam santaH yoginaH vEzNavAH taTA /
   jyotir-abhyantare rūpam atulaṃ śyāma-sundaram // Jss_1,1.3 //	jyotiH--aByantare rUpam atulam SyAma--sundaram // JsH-_1,1.3 //
   dhyāyet taṃ paramaṃ brahma paramātmānam īśvaram /	DyAyet tam paramam brahma paramAtmAnam ISvaram /
   nirīham ati-nirliptam nirguṇaṃ prakṛteḥ paraṃ // Jss_1,1.4 //	nirIham ati-nirliptam nirguNam prakRteH param // JsH-_1,1.4 //
   sarveśaṃ sarva-rūpaṃ ca sarva-kāraṇa-kāraṇam /	sarva-ISam sarva-rUpam ca sarva-kAraNa--kAraNam /

   maṅgalyaṃ maṅgalārhaṃ ca maṅgalaṃ maṅgalālayam /	maFgalyam maFgala-arham ca maFgalam maFgala-Alayam /

   stuvanti vedā yaṃ śaśvann ānantaṃ jānanti yasya te /	stuvanti vedAH yam SaSvan Anantam jAnanti yasya te /
   taṃ staumi paramānandaṃ sānandaṃ nanda-nandanam // Jss_1,1.7 //	tam stOmi parama-Anandam sa-Anandam nanda--nandanam // JsH-_1,1.7 //
   bhakta-priyaṃ ca bhakteśaṃ bhaktānugraha-vigrahaṃ /	Bakta-priyam ca BakteSam Bakta-anugraha-vigraham /
   śrīdaṃ śrīśaṃ śrī-nivāsaṃ śrī-kṛṣṇaṃ rādhikeśvaram // Jss_1,1.8 //	SrIdam SrISam SrI--nivAsam SrI--kRzNam rADikeSvaram // JsH-_1,1.8 //
   jñānāmṛtaṃ jñāna-sindhoḥ saṃprāpya śaṅkarād guroḥ /	jQAna-amRtam jQAna-sinDoH saMprApya SaFkarAt guroH /
   parāvarāc ca paramād yogīndrāṇāṃ guror guroḥ // Jss_1,1.9 //	parAvarAt ca paramAt yogi-indrANAm guroH guroH // JsH-_1,1.9 //
   vedebhyo dadhi-sindhubhyaś caturbhyaḥ sumanoharam /	vedeByaH daDi-sinDuByaH caturByaH su-manoharam /
   taj jñāna-mantha-daṇḍena saṃnirmathya navaṃ navam // Jss_1,1.10 //	tat jQAna-manTa--daNxena saMnirmaTya navam navam // JsH-_1,1.10 //
   navanītaṃ samuddhṛtya natvā śambhoḥ padāmbujam /	navanItam samudDRtya natvA SamBoH pada-ambujam /
   vidhi-putro nārado 'haṃ pañca-rātraṃ samārabhe // Jss_1,1.11 //	viDi-putraH nAradaH aham paQca--rAtram samAraBe // JsH-_1,1.11 //
   oṃ nārāyaṇāśrame puṇye puṇya-kṣetre ca bhārata /	om nArAyaNa-ASrame puNye puNya-kzetre ca BArata /
   siddhe nārāyaṇa-kṣetre vaṭa-mūle supuṇyade // Jss_1,1.12 //	sidDe nArAyaNa-kzetre vawa--mUle su-puNya-de // JsH-_1,1.12 //
   kṛṣṇāṃśaṃ kṛṣṇa-bhaktaṃ ca palaṃ kṛṣṇa-parāyaṇam /	kRzNa-aMSam kRzNa-Baktam ca palam kRzNa--parAyaNam /
   śrī-kṛṣṇa-caraṇāmbhoja-dhyānaikatāna-mānasam // Jss_1,1.13 //	SrI-kRzNa--caraNa-amBoja--DyAna-eka-tAna--mAnasam // JsH-_1,1.13 //
   japantaṃ paramaṃ brahma kṛṣṇa ity akṣara-dvayam /	japantam paramam brahma kRzNaH iti akzara--dvayam /
   sukhāsane sukhāsīnaṃ kṛṣṇa-dvaipāyanaṃ munim // Jss_1,1.14 //	suKa-Asane suKa-AsInam kRzNa--dvEpAyanam munim // JsH-_1,1.14 //
   papraccha śukadevaś ca sarva-jñaṃ pitaraṃ muniḥ /	papracCa SukadevaH ca sarva-jQam pitaram muniH /
   kāraṇaṇ ca purāṇānāṃ purāṇaṃ param avyayam // Jss_1,1.15 //	kAraNaN ca purANAnAm purANam param avyayam // JsH-_1,1.15 //
   śrī-śuka uvāca	SrI-SukaH uvAca

   yad yat prakāraṃ jñānaṃ ca nigūḍhaṃ śruti-sammatam // Jss_1,1.16 //	yat yat prakAram jQAnam ca nigUXam Sruti--sammatam // JsH-_1,1.16 //

   tat tat sarvaṃ samālocya māṃ bodhayitum arhasi // Jss_1,1.17 //	tat tat sarvam samAlocya mAm boDayitum arhasi // JsH-_1,1.17 //
   atha śrī-kṛṣṇa-bhakti-praśaṃśā	aTa SrI--kRzNa--Bakti--praSaMSA

   sā bhaktiḥ paramā śuddhā kṛṣṇa-dāsya-pradā ca yā // Jss_1,1.18 //	sA BaktiH paramA SudDA kRzNa-dAsya--pradA ca yAH // JsH-_1,1.18 //
   tad eva dāsyaṃ śastaṃ yat sākṣāc caraṇa-sevanaṃ /	tat eva dAsyam Sastam yat sAkzAt caraNa-sevanam /
   nityaṃ goloka-vāsaṃ ca purataḥ stavanaṃ hareḥ // Jss_1,1.19 //	nityam goloka--vAsam ca puratas stavanam hareH // JsH-_1,1.19 //
   śaśvan nimeṣa-rahitaṃ tat-pāda-padma-darśanam /	SaSvat nimeza--rahitam tat-pAda--padma--darSanam /
   śaśvat tat-sārdham ālāpa-sevā-karma-niyojanam // Jss_1,1.20 //	SaSvat tat-sA-arDam AlApa--sevA--karma--niyojanam // JsH-_1,1.20 //
   tena sārdham aviccheda-sthānaṃ paraṃ śobhanam /	tena sArDam avicCeda--sTAnam param SoBanam /
   bhaktānāṃ vāñcchitaṃ vastu sāra-bhūtaṃ śrutau śrutam // Jss_1,1.21 //	BaktAnAm vAQcCitam vastu sAra-BUtam SrutO Srutam // JsH-_1,1.21 //
   putrasya vacanaṃ śrutvā vyāsadevo jahāsa saḥ /	putrasya vacanam SrutvA vyAsa-devaH jahAsa saH /
   vijñāya jñāninaṃ putraṃ paramāhlādam āpa ha // Jss_1,1.22 //	vijQAya jQAninam putram parama-AhlAdam Apa ha // JsH-_1,1.22 //
   putraṃ śubhāśiṣaṃ kṛtvā sarva-jñaḥ sarva-bhāvanaḥ /	putram SuBa-ASizam kRtvA sarva-jQaH sarva--BAvanaH /
   yathāprāptaṃ guru-mukhāt pravaktum upacakrame // Jss_1,1.23 //	yaTAprAptam guru-muKAt pravaktum upacakrame // JsH-_1,1.23 //

   sodarān bāndhavāṃś caiva bhṛtyān patnīṃ sahātmajām // Jss_1,1.26 //	sodarAn bAnDavAn ca-eva BRtyAn patnIm saha-AtmajAm // JsH-_1,1.26 //

   siddhā maharṣayaś ca munayaḥ sankādayaḥ // Jss_1,15.7 //	sidDAH mahA-RzayaH ca munayaH sanka-AdayaH // JsH-_1,15.7 //
   yogīndrā jñāninaḥ sarve samūcuḥ śambhu-saṃsadi /	yogi-indrAH jQAninaH sarve samUcuH SamBu--saMsadi /
   yat stotraṃ kavacaṃ dhyānaṃ subhadrāya ca kānane // Jss_1,15.8 //	yat stotram kavacam DyAnam suBadrAya ca kAnane // JsH-_1,15.8 //
   nārāyaṇarṣi-bhagavān brāhmaṇāya dadau purā /	nArAyaNa-Rzi--BagavAn brAhmaNAya dadO purA /
   pūjā-vidhānaṃ yad yac ca puraś-caraṇa-pūrvakam // Jss_1,15.9 //	pUjA--viDAnam yat yat ca puraS-caraNa--pUrvakam // JsH-_1,15.9 //
   tad eva bhagavān śambhuḥ pradadau nāradāya ca /	tat eva BagavAn SamBuH pradadO nAradAya ca /
   uvāca śambhuṃ devarṣir yogināṃ ca guror gurum /	uvAca SamBum devarziH yoginAm ca guroH gurum /
   pārvatī-sannidhau tatra nāradaś ca mahā-muniḥ // Jss_1,15.10 //	pArvatI--sanniDO tatra nAradaH ca mahA--muniH // Jss_1,15.10 //
   bhagavan sarva-dharma-jña sarva-jña sarva-kāraṇa /	Bagavan sarva--Darma-jQa sarva-jQa sarva-kAraNa /
   sad yat pṛṣṭaṃ mayā pūrvaṃ tan māṃ vyākhyātum arhasi // Jss_1,15.11 //	sat yat pRzwam mayA pUrvam tat mAm vyAKyAtum arhasi // JsH-_1,15.11 //
   yad yat pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā brahman pratyekaṃ ca krameṇa ca /	yat yat pRzwam tvayA brahman pratyekam ca krameNa ca /
   punaḥ praśnaṃ kuru mune śṛṇvantu mat-sabhāsadaḥ // Jss_1,15.12 //	punar praSnam kuru mune SRNvantu mat--saBAsadaH // JsH-_1,15.12 //
   ādhyātmikaṃ ca yaj jñānaṃ vedānāṃ sāram uttamam /	ADyAtmikam ca yat jQAnam vedAnAm sAram uttamam /
   jñānaṃ jñāniṣu sāraṃ yat kṛṣṇa-bhakti-pradaṃ śubhaṃ // Jss_1,15.13 //	jQAnam jQAnizu sAram yat kRzNa--Bakti--pradam SuBam // JsH-_1,15.13 //
   nirvāṇa-muktidaṃ jñānaṃ karma-mūla-nikṛntanam /	nirvANa--mukti-dam jQAnam karma--mUla-nikRntanam /
   tat-siddhi-yogān muktiś ca yoginām api vāñcchitam // Jss_1,15.14 //	tat-sidDi--yogAt muktiH ca yoginAm api vAQcCitam // JsH-_1,15.14 //
   saṃsāra-viṣayaṃ jñānaṃ śaśvat sammoha-veṣṭitam /	saMsAra--vizayam jQAnam SaSvat sammoha-vezwitam /
   āśramāṇāṃ samācāraṃ teṣāṃ dharma-pariṣkṛtam // Jss_1,15.15 //	ASramANAm samAcAram tezAm Darma-parizkRtam // JsH-_1,15.15 //
   caturṇāṃ varṇanāṃ vidhānāṃ maheśvara /	caturNAm varNanAm viDAnAm maheSvaraH /
   bhikṣūṇāṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ ca yatīnāṃ brahma-cāriṇām // Jss_1,15.16 //	BikzUNAm vEzNavAnAm ca yatInAm brahma-cAriNAm // JsH-_1,15.16 //
   vāna-prasthāśramāṇāṃ ca paṇḍitānāṃ tathaiva ca /	vAna--prasTa-ASramANAm ca paNxitAnAm taTA-eva ca /
   pati-vratānāṃ yad yac ca śrī-kṛṣṇa-pūjanaṃ ca yat // Jss_1,15.17 //	pati-vratAnAm yat yat ca SrI--kRzNa--pUjanam ca yat // JsH-_1,15.17 //
   yat stotraṃ kavacaṃ mantraṃ puraś-caraṇam īpsitam /	yat stotram kavacam mantram puraS-caraNam Ipsitam /
   sārvāhnikam abhīṣṭaṃ ca vipākaṃ karma-jīvinām // Jss_1,15.18 //	sArvAhnikam aBIzwam ca vipAkam karma--jIvinAm // JsH-_1,15.18 //
   saṃsāra-vāsanā-baddhaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ prakṛtīśayoḥ /	saMsAra--vAsanA--badDam lakzaNam prakRti-ISayoH /
   tayoḥ paraṃ vā yad brahma tasyāvatāra-varṇanam // Jss_1,15.19 //	tayoH param vA yat brahma tasya-avatAra-varNanam // JsH-_1,15.19 //
   kas tat kalāvatīrṇaś ca kas tad-aṃśaś tathaiva ca /	kaH tat kalA-avatIrNaH ca kaH tad--aMSaH taTA-eva ca /
   paripūrṇatamaḥ kaś ca kaḥ pūrṇaḥ kaḥ kalāṃśakaḥ // Jss_1,15.20 //	paripUrNatamaH kaH ca kaH pUrNaH kaH kalA-aMSakaH // JsH-_1,15.20 //
   kasya vārādhane śambho kiṃ phalaṃ kiṃ yaśas tathā /	kasya vA-ArADane SamBo kim Palam kim yaSaH taTA /

   nārāyaṇarṣi-kavacaṃ subhadra-brāhmaṇāya ca /	nArAyaNa-Rzi--kavacam suBadra--brAhmaNAya ca /

   ati-saṃgopanīyaṃ ca kavacaṃ paramādbhutam /	ati-saMgopanIyam ca kavacam parama-adButam /

   sanat-kumāro jānāti noktaṃ tena purā ca mām /	sanat-kumAraH jAnAti na-uktam tena purA ca mAm /
   mayā jñānam anāpṛṣṭaṃ yad yaj jānāsi maṅgalam // Jss_1,15.24 //	mayA jQAnam anApRzwam yat yat jAnAsi maFgalam // JsH-_1,15.24 //
   veda-sāram anupamaṃ karma-mūla-nikṛntanam /	veda--sAram anupamam karma--mUla-nikRntanam /
   tan me kathaya bhadreśa mām evānugrahaṃ kuru // Jss_1,15.25 //	tat me kaTaya BadreSa mAm eva-anugraham kuru // JsH-_1,15.25 //
   apūrvaṃ rādhikākhyānaṃ vedeṣu ca sudurlabham /	apUrvam rADikA-AKyAnam vedezu ca su-durlaBam /

   guroś ca jñānodigaraṇāt jñānaṃ syān mantra-tantrayoḥ /	guroH ca jQAna-udigaraNAt jQAnam syAt mantra-tantrayoH /

   jñānaṃ syād viduṣāṃ kiṃcid veda-vyākhyānataḥ prabho /	jQAnam syAt viduzAm kiMcid veda--vyAKyAnataH praBo /
   veda-kāraṇa-pūjyaś tvaṃ jñānādhiṣṭhātṛ-devatā // Jss_1,15.28 //	veda--kAraNa--pUjyaH tvam jQAna-aDizWAtR-devatAH // Jss_1,15.28 //

   hari-bhakti-pradaṃ sarvaṃ karma-mūla-nikṛntanam // Jss_1,15.31 //	hari--Bakti-pradam sarvam karma--mUla-nikRntanam // JsH-_1,15.31 //
   iti śrī-nārada-pañca-rātre jñānāmṛta-sāre	iti SrI-nArada--paQca-rAtre jQAna-amRta--sAre
